< Review>
Even tho it says they open at 9am during the week it never seems to be open until like 10am. Everyone who works there is very pleasant. It gets busy during lunch time and I would say also around after 5p. They have 4 delivery drivers, 2 cooks and 2 front counter employees.
They have about 6 selections on beer to go with any pizza that you decide on. They have inside seating with 3 giant TV's that always have some sports playing , and some outside patio tables with chairs for those who enjoy people watching while they eat. They do close at 10p but on fri-sat they close at 11.< /Review>

<Rating>3</Rating>< Review>
This location used to be another Filipino restaurant called ‚ÄúSarap‚Äù. Came here today and was surprised that the name ‚Äúchanged‚Äù to ‚ÄúSarap‚Äù but it was later confirmed by one of the servers that it is a completely different restaurant. It was a Sunday Bruch, there was fairly good amount of customers but unfortunately there were only 2 servers working the floor. Our server was nice but it was very obvious that she is overwhelmed and made a comment ‚Äúoh we‚Äôre popular today!‚Äù (Don‚Äôt know what she meant by this but we just played along and placed the order). We were given a brunch menu...very limited choices and I think they could either lower the price or make the servings commensurate to the cost of the meal. We got Adobo Fried Chicken with Ube Waffle-$15(3 pieces of fried chicken with 1 purple yam flavored waffle that was cut into 4). Since this is a Filipino fusion restaurant, I wasn‚Äôt really expecting the real deal adobo but to be honest, the chicken was very under seasoned. The waffle was ok though but could be better. Overall the meal was underwhelming and dry, I think there should be a side of sauce/gravy/syrup or something to complement this meal.

I know that the restaurant just opened 1 month ago and they‚Äôre probably still working out the kinks. I really do have high hopes for this restaurant and it is about time to have a quality Filipino restaurant in town. I am hoping that they will listen to reviews and make improvements. For sure will be back, but probably will wait for a bit.</Review>

<userid>107956764052321074558</userid><Name>Jon V.< /Name><Date>1550183907536< /Date><Rate>4< /Rate><Text>Reviewed on 2018-11-11

Abbreviated the place to SFK for simplification purposes.  Located on Miramar Rd. across from the Marine Corps Air Station.

The calamari is the best.  It's flavorful and the squid was delightfully tender.

The Sisig, made from parts of pig head and liver, was served on a sizzling platter, filled with saut√©ed chopped onions.  It came with an over easy egg yolk to be mixed with the Sisig soon after it curdles.  The best Sisig I've had in a while.  Note that this is a unique Pinoy's delicacy and could take some time for some who have not had this food to acquire the taste.

The fried marinated milkfish was thick and came with sliced tomatoes and fresh mangos.

The pansit palabok (noodles) sauce was a little bland.

The restaurant is spacious and decorated to fulfill the humble feeling of a Bahay Kubo, a Nipa hut, equipped with dark walnut finished tables.  There are also bar tables around the corner to enjoy the cocktail selections.

Loyd our server is amazing and has a sense of humor.

The bathroom is clean and stylish.

We'll visit again in the future.</Text><Pics>None<//Pics>< Resp>

< review>
We shopped around for a climate-controlled space for some household items due to our pending "downsizing" to an apartment from a house.  We chose ESS Palm Desert due to its pricing.  When we arrived, we found that that there was a computer glitch concerning our online reservation.  However, Stephanie, the Assistant Manager, was quick to the rescue and saved the day!  Her care and concern actually allowed us to secure an even more appropriate unit for the same price.  She even made the entire process fun!  We felt like she truly cared about our storage needs, and wanted to make sure we were happy.  Although we live in Palm Springs, we gladly will make the short hop to Palm Desert in order to store our belongs at this particular place, knowing that Stephanie is there.< /review>
